healthcoachjourney.com

Privacy Policy

Because your trust and privacy matter.

1. Introduction

Welcome to healthcoachjourney.com. This Privacy Policy explains how we collect, use, and protect your information when you visit this website. By using this site, you agree to the terms outlined in this policy.

This website is an independent personal project and not affiliated with or endorsed by the Institute for Integrative Nutrition (IIN) or any other organization.

2. Information We Collect

  • Send us an email or fill out a contact form
  • Subscribe to updates or newsletters (if available)
  • Click on affiliate or referral links

The types of information may include your name, email address, and general analytics data (such as page views or time on site) via tools like Google Analytics.

3. How We Use Your Information

  • Respond to your inquiries or feedback
  • Improve website content and functionality
  • Track anonymous traffic data
  • Maintain affiliate reporting (where applicable)

We do not sell, rent, or share your personal data with third parties for marketing purposes.

4. Cookies

This website may use cookies to improve user experience and analyze traffic. You can disable cookies in your browser settings. Some affiliate or analytics services may also use cookies to track referral activity in a privacy-compliant way.

5. Affiliate Links

Some articles may contain affiliate links. When you click on these links and make a purchase, we may receive a small commission at no extra cost to you.

These programs use cookies to correctly attribute referrals and track commissions. All affiliate partnerships are disclosed transparently.

6. Data Security

We take reasonable steps to protect your information from unauthorized access. However, please note that no online transmission can be guaranteed as 100% secure.

Who I Am

Hi, Iâ€™m Chen Jinmei (Naijian Lin) â€” a certified graduate of the Institute for Integrative Nutrition (IIN) and a holistic health coach based in California. My background began in the corporate world, where I spent years working long hours with little balance. Over time, I realized I wanted to help others improve their energy, relationships, and overall well-being through practical, compassionate coaching.

This website is my personal blog â€” a space where I share my honest reflections on health coaching, learning experiences, and the lessons I gained during my studies at IIN. Everything here is written from my own perspective as a former student and practicing health coach.

My Mission

My goal is simple: to share real experiences, helpful resources, and inspiration for people who are exploring health coaching or looking to make positive lifestyle changes. I believe wellness is not about perfection â€” itâ€™s about progress, awareness, and kindness to ourselves and others.

Disclaimer

Transparency and integrity are at the heart of everything shared on this site.

1. Independent Personal Website

healthcoachjourney.com is an independent, personally operated website created for the purpose of sharing educational content and personal experiences related to health coaching, holistic wellness, and professional growth.

This site is not affiliated with, endorsed by, or officially connected to the Institute for Integrative Nutrition (IIN) or any other institution mentioned. All opinions and reflections expressed are entirely those of the author.

2. Educational and Informational Purposes Only

The content on this website is provided for educational and informational purposes only. It should not be interpreted as professional medical advice, diagnosis, or treatment. Always seek the advice of your physician or other qualified health provider regarding any questions you may have about a medical condition or health goals.

3. Affiliate Links & Transparency

Some pages on this site may include affiliate links or referral links. This means that if you choose to make a purchase or register through those links, the author may receive a small commission at no additional cost to you.

These links help support the cost of maintaining the website and creating free educational content. However, all opinions expressed are genuine and based on personal experience, not influenced by compensation.

4. Accuracy of Information

While every effort is made to ensure the accuracy and timeliness of information shared here, healthcoachjourney.com makes no warranties or guarantees regarding completeness, reliability, or suitability of the information provided. Readers are encouraged to verify information directly from official or primary sources when making decisions.

5. External Links

This site may contain links to other websites for convenience and informational purposes. healthcoachjourney.com does not control or assume responsibility for the content, accuracy, or practices of external sites.

6. Contact

For any questions regarding this disclaimer or the content on this site, please contact: chenjinmei51@gmail.com.

Privacy Policy

Because your trust and privacy matter.

1. Introduction

Welcome to healthcoachjourney.com. This Privacy Policy explains how we collect, use, and protect your information when you visit this website. By using this site, you agree to the terms outlined in this policy.

This website is an independent personal project and not affiliated with or endorsed by the Institute for Integrative Nutrition (IIN) or any other organization.

2. Information We Collect

We only collect information that you voluntarily provide, such as when you:

  • Send us an email or fill out a contact form
  • Subscribe to updates or newsletters (if available)
  • Click on affiliate or referral links

The types of information may include your name, email address, and general non-identifiable analytics data (such as page views or time on site) via tools like Google Analytics.

3. How We Use Your Information

The information collected is used to:

  • Respond to your inquiries or feedback
  • Improve website content and functionality
  • Track anonymous traffic data to understand site performance
  • Maintain affiliate program reporting (where applicable)

We do not sell, rent, or share your personal data with third parties for marketing purposes.

4. Cookies

This website may use cookiesâ€”small text files stored on your deviceâ€”to improve user experience and analyze traffic. You can disable cookies in your browser settings at any time. Some affiliate or analytics services may also use cookies to track referral activity in a privacy-compliant way.

5. Affiliate Links

Some articles may contain affiliate or referral links. When you click on these links and make a purchase, we may receive a small commission at no extra cost to you. These programs use cookies to correctly attribute referrals and track commissions.

All affiliate partnerships are disclosed transparently, and we only promote products or services aligned with our mission of supporting wellness and education.

6. Data Security

We take reasonable steps to protect your personal information from unauthorized access or disclosure. However, please note that no data transmission over the Internet can be guaranteed as 100% secure.

7. Your Rights

You have the right to request access, correction, or deletion of your personal information. To make such a request, please contact us at chenjinmei51@gmail.com.

8. Updates to This Policy

This Privacy Policy may be updated periodically to reflect changes in legal requirements or website practices. Any updates will be posted on this page with a revised effective date.

9. Contact

If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy or your data, please reach out to: chenjinmei51@gmail.com
